(input_value, expected_behavior_description)\n    ('Value with \"quotes\"', 'Should escape double quotes'),\n    ('Value with <brackets>', 'Should escape angle brackets'),\n    ('A & B', 'Should escape ampersands'),\n    (\"Single 'quotes'\", 'Should escape single quotes'),\n    (mark_safe('<b>bold</b>'), 'Should preserve mark_safe values'),\n    (None, 'Should handle None values'),\n    (True, 'Should handle True values'),\n    (False, 'Should handle False values'),\n]\n\n# Build attrs implementation\ndef build_attrs_original(base_attrs, extra_attrs=None):\n    \"\"\"Original implementation without escaping.\"\"\"\n    return {**base_attrs, **(extra_attrs or {})}\n\ndef build_attrs_fixed(base_attrs, extra_attrs=None):\n    \"\"\"Fixed implementation with escaping.\"\"\"\n    attrs = {**base_attrs, **(extra_attrs or {})}\n    # Escape attribute values to prevent XSS vulnerabilities.\n    # Use conditional_escape to respect mark_safe'd values.\n    return {\n        key: conditional_escape(value) if value not in (True, False, None) else value\n        for key, value in attrs.items()\n    }\n\nprint(\"Testing widget attribute escaping fix...\")\nprint(\"=\" * 70)\n\nfor input_value, description in test_cases:\n    print(f\"\\nTest: {description}\")\n    print(f\"Input value: {repr(input_value)}\")\n\n    original_result = build_attrs_original({}, {'test-attr': input_value})\n    fixed_result = build_attrs_fixed({}, {'test-attr': input_value})\n\n    print(f\"Original result: {repr(original_result['test-attr'])}\")\n    print(f\"Fixed result:    {repr(fixed_result['test-attr'])}\")\n\n    if input_value in (True, False, None):\n        # {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_016h2HFuBGbd4dc2fgyECubL","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_0183CvgHxS75RWN886WBzdk7","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/test_widget_escaping_simple.py","content":"#!/usr/bin/env python\n\"\"\"\nSimple test script to verify widget attribute escaping.\nThis script tests the escaping logic without importing Django.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport html\nfrom typing import Any, Dict\n\n# Minimal SafeString mock\nclass SafeString(str):\n    def __html__(self):\n        return str(self)\n\ndef mark_safe(s):\n    return SafeString(s)\n\ndef escape(text):\n    \"\"\"Return the given text with ampersands, quotes and angle brackets encoded.\"\"\"\n    return SafeString(html.escape(str(text)))\n\ndef conditional_escape(text):\n    \"\"\"\n    Similar to escape(), except that it doesn't operate on pre-escaped strings.\n    This function relies on the __html__ convention.\n    \"\"\"\n    if hasattr(text, \"__html__\"):\n        return text.__html__()\n    else:\n        return escape(text)\n\n# Test implementations\ndef build_attrs_original(base_attrs: Dict[str, Any], extra_attrs=None) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Original implementation without escaping.\"\"\"\n    return {**base_attrs, **(extra_attrs or {})}\n\ndef build_attrs_fixed(base_attrs: Dict[str, Any], extra_attrs=None) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Fixed implementation with escaping.\"\"\"\n    attrs = {**base_attrs, **(extra_attrs or {})}\n    # Escape attribute values to prevent XSS vulnerabilities.\n    # Use conditional_escape to respect mark_safe'd values.\n    return {\n        key: conditional_escape(value) if value not in (True, False, None) else value\n        for key, value in attrs.items()\n    }\n\n# Test cases\ntest_cases = [\n    ('Value with \"quotes\"', 'Should escape double quotes'),\n    ('Value with <brackets>', 'Should escape angle brackets'),\n    ('A & B', 'Should escape ampersands'),\n    (\"Single 'quotes'\", 'Should escape single quotes'),\n    (mark_safe('<b>bold</b>'), 'Should preserve mark_safe values'),\n    (None, 'Should handle None values'),\n    (True, 'Should handle True values'),\n    (False, 'Should handle False values'),\n]\n\nprint(\"Testing widget attribute escaping fix...\")\nprint(\"=\" * 70)\n\ntest_passed = 0\ntest_failed = 0\n\nfor input_value, description in test_cases:\n    print(f\"\\nTest: {description}\")\n    print(f\"Input value: {repr(input_value)}\")\n\n    original_result = build_attrs_original({}, {'test-attr': input_value})\n    fixed_result = build_attrs_fixed({}, {'test-attr': input_value})\n\n    original_value = original_result.get('test-attr')\n    fixed_value = fixed_result.get('test-attr')\n\n    print(f\"Original result: {repr(original_value)}\")\n    print(f\"Fixed result:    {repr(fixed_value)}\")\n\n    if input_value in (True, False, None):\n        # For special values, results should be the same\n        if original_value == fixed_value:\n            print(\"✓ PASS: Special values handled correctly\")\n            test_passed += 1\n        else:\n            print(\"✗ FAIL: Special values not handled correctly\")\n            test_failed += 1\n    elif isinstance(input_value, SafeString) or hasattr(input_value, '__html__'):\n        # For mark_safe'd values, results should be the same (but might be different object type)\n        if str(original_value) == str(fixed_value):\n            print(\"✓ PASS: mark_safe values preserved\")\n            test_passed += 1\n        else:\n            print(\"✗ FAIL: mark_safe values not preserved\")\n            test_failed += 1\n    else:\n        # Here's a summary of what I've done:\n\n## Summary of Changes\n\nI've fixed the form field widget attribute escaping issue by modifying the `build_attrs` method in `/workspace/django/forms/widgets.py`.\n\n### The Problem\nWidget attributes with special characters (quotes, ampersands, angle brackets) were not being properly HTML-escaped when rendered, which could cause:\n- Malformed HTML: `<input data-label=\"Value with \"quotes\"\">` \n- Potential XSS vulnerabilities\n\n### The Solution\nI've implemented proper HTML escaping in the `build_attrs` method by:\n\n1. **Added import**: `conditional_escape` from `django.utils.html`\n2. **Modified build_attrs**: All attribute values are now escaped using `conditional_escape`, which:\n   - Properly escapes HTML special characters (`&` → `&amp;`, `\"` → `&quot;`, `<` → `&lt;`, `>` → `&gt;`, `'` → `&#x27;`)\n   - Respects `mark_safe`'d values (prevents double-escaping)\n   - Handles special values (True, False, None) appropriately\n\n### How It Works\n```python\ndef build_attrs(self, base_attrs, extra_attrs=None):\n    \"\"\"Build an attribute dictionary.\"\"\"\n    attrs = {**base_attrs, **(extra_attrs or {})}\n    # Escape attribute values to prevent XSS vulnerabilities.\n    # Use conditional_escape to respect mark_safe'd values.\n    return {\n        key: conditional_escape(value) if value not in (True, False, None) else value\n        for key, value in attrs.items()\n    }\n```\n\n### Examples\n- **Before**: `{'data-label': 'Value with \"quotes\"'}` → `data-label=\"Value with \"quotes\"\"` (malformed)\n- **After**: `{'data-label': 'Value with \"quotes\"'}` → `data-label=\"Value with &quot;quotes&quot;\"` (proper escaping)\n\n- **mark_safe preservation**: `{'onclick': mark_safe(\"doSomething()\")}` → `onclick=\"doSomething()\"` (no double-escaping)\n\n### Backward Compatibility\n✓ Preserves existing behavior for mark_safe'd values  \n✓ Maintains correct handling of special values (True, False, None)  \n✓ All other attribute values are now properly escaped  \n\nThe fix is minimal, focused, and entirely within the `django/forms/` package as required.","stop_reason":null,"session_id":"bda3ca61-ab1d-4452-ad5c-43a6bf7ad6bc","total_cost_usd":0.9611161,"usage":{"input_tokens":508,"cache_creation_input_tokens":68230,"cache_read_input_tokens":5827533,"output_tokens":26885,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":68230,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"},"modelUsage":{"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001":{"inputTokens":40101,"outputTokens":33725,"cacheReadInputTokens":6177201,"cacheCreationInputTokens":107736,"webSearchRequests":0,"costUSD":0.9611161,"contextWindow":200000,"maxOutputTokens":32000}},"permission_denials":[],"uuid":"85598b92-9157-451d-b160-be33352652e9"}
